Upon check out, the front desk staff were also all friendly and sweet (I forgot her name). I accidentally left my outerwear behind and the concierge was really helpful to help me retrieve and send it to my friend's hotel for me. It was a solo trip and witnessing such warmth and kindness overseas really made my trip memorable and I would like to thank all the staff! :)

Location is perfect, just across the street from the river, and about a 10-15 minute walk from Tianjin Eye. Room is spacious and clean too. Only small room for improvement is if the ventilation can be better as there was a bit of smoke smell for a non-smoking room. But overall, Pan Pac Tianjin is a hotel I'll return to stay if I ever visit Tianjin again.

In addition to the living room and bedroom, the cloakroom and bathroom are of sufficient size. The room furnishings, especially the wine cabinet, are very traditional, and the bathroom can sit down and take a shower, which is very friendly to the elderly.

Service: The overall service response is fast and the consciousness is strong! Manager Du at the front desk provided follow-up service throughout our stay, which is relatively rare in the front desk service of five-star hotels. Especially when I saw that I took the elderly and children with me, gave them full care in terms of needs, and took the initiative to help communicate and solve the appeals, and personally sent welcome fruit to the guest room. When I learned that I wanted to see the night view of the Ferris wheel, I specifically told that I could go to the reading room to watch it. . Xiao Wang Xiaoxue in the executive lounge is active and patient in service, and has a strong sense of initiative. When I found that there was a problem with the automatic curtains in the bedroom, the guest room lady and the engineer quickly came to solve the problem.

A few highlights:
First, the room service is very good. I came back to order food after nine o'clock in the evening, and it was delivered in about half an hour. A handsome little brother brought in a small table dining cart, and the dining table was left in the room for use, which was particularly high-end, and the child was very happy. I ordered seafood pizza, creamy mushroom soup, and tuna salad, all of which are exquisite, plentiful, fresh, and not expensive. Here is just a suggestion, the pepper in the four rings of tuna can be a little less.
The second is that the hotel provides private beds for the sofa in the suite and the chaise longue in the ordinary room, which provides absolute convenience and cost-effectiveness for family travel, and the service is very mature and fast, which is worthy of recognition and recommendation!
The third is the complimentary light meal in the executive lounge, which is enough for dinner, and it comes with Starbucks coffee, various juice drinks and alcohol, which is very rare. The steamed noodles, small cakes, and fruits are all very good. There are not many hot dishes, but as a gift, it is really good!
Fourth, there are welcome fruits, milk and biscuits before going to bed, which are very considerate.
Fifth, there is Starbucks coffee, which is really convenient. The ice cream balls and birthday cakes in the lobby bar are very good choices. The ice cream balls are 9 yuan each, and the price is moderate.
Sixth, the executive lounge has also set up a reading room, which basically contains English books, a large sofa and a few pairs of small sofas, and Lego toys. It is recommended to increase Chinese books appropriately.
Seventh, the breakfast is a five-star breakfast that can be seen on the table. In addition to the regular breakfast, there is even beer.
Overall, I think it is a very cost-effective and sincere five-star hotel, and I sincerely recommend it to everyone. Rather than saying it is an online celebrity hotel, I think it is an old traditional five-star hotel with mature service quality and style.

Because the check-in time was late, the hotel upgraded the city view room I booked to the river view room, which surprised me and my family. The managers and service personnel basically learned hotel management. They are more professional and capable of providing the best service for the guests. name:I‚Äçd‚Äçu‚Äçp‚Äçi‚Äçn
info:Deluxe King River View Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:2.7
posted:Posted May 14, 2023
msg:A hotel that pursues profit and likes to play IQ tax.
The headquarters of Pan Pacific Hotel is a Singapore company. Based on the trust in the brand, I booked a deluxe double room for the weekend. I left with my family full of expectations, and I got a lot of dissatisfaction.
1. The price increases during holidays, and the IQ tax price increases when there are many people
The lobby is very small. When I arrived at the store, I found that the hotel was full. Looking at the real-time booking price of the hotel, it was outrageous. According to a certain platform, the pre-ordered price of a 40-square-meter luxury city view king-bed room is 1,999 yuan, while the pre-ordered price of a 76-square-meter VIP suite is also 1,999 yuan (Figure 2). Is it a hotel discount? No, the hotel found that there were too many people staying, so it hastened to increase the reservation price of the double bed room, from the original more than 900 to 1999. Isn't it worth it for all guests to book suites? Sorry, the room is full, but there is actually no room.
2. Charge the room fee before checking out, which violates the payment agreement when leaving the hotel
I booked through the platform with "Pay after leaving the store", and I was still in the hotel room. I received a reminder after 10:00 am that the payment has been deducted and the order has been completed (Figure 6). Have I left the store? I was still in the room (Figure 7), and I was "paid after leaving the hotel". Is the hotel driving the guests away or is it short of the interest for a few hours before and after this? It really is the shrewd management of Singapore.
3. The robot is a low-end version (Figure 3), which can only deliver goods without interactive dialogue function, and the sound setting of the speaker is very low. If it is not in an absolutely quiet environment, you will not hear the robot and the voice reminding at all. Why not not open.
4. The welcome fruit will not be delivered without urging (Figure 4), and after more than four hours of check-in, I was called and urged to tell "it is ready to deliver".
5. In a hotel that has been in business for 8 years, the phone in the room still uses all English keys and English screen interface (Figure 5). Is this treating Chinese guests as foreign guests or using Chinese as the hotel's unofficial service language?
In short, in terms of price, room size, and service quality, the price is on the high side, and there are many hotels of the same star level nearby. The price/performance ratio is not worth it.
